The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            if (!node.isTryWithResources()) {
                addViolation(data, tryBlock);
            } else {
                for (ASTResource resource : node.findChildrenOfType(ASTResource.class)) {
                    ASTVariableDeclaratorId variableDeclaratorId = resource.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
                    if (variableDeclaratorId != null && !"ignored".equals(variableDeclaratorId.getName())) {
                        addViolation(data, tryBlock);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            if (!node.isTryWithResources()) {
                addViolation(data, tryBlock);
            } else {
                for (ASTResource resource : node.findChildrenOfType(ASTResource.class)) {
                    ASTVariableDeclaratorId variableDeclaratorId = resource.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
                    if (variableDeclaratorId != null && !"ignored".equals(variableDeclaratorId.getName())) {
                        addViolation(data, tryBlock);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            if (!node.isTryWithResources()) {
                addViolation(data, tryBlock);
            } else {
                ASTResourceList resourceList = node.getResourceList();
                if (resourceList != null) {
                    for (ASTResource resource : resourceList.children(ASTResource.class)) {
                        ASTVariableDeclaratorId varDeclId = resource.getFirstDescendantOfType(ASTVariableDeclaratorId.class);
                        if (varDeclId != null && !"ignored".equals(varDeclId.getName())) {
                            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTBlock.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock body = node.getBody();
        if (body != null && body.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 0 && node.getParent() instanceof ASTInitializer) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        } else if (node.isTryWithResources() && tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        if (node.isTryWithResources() && tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

===============================新加一个测试用例生成的checker repair_test_error_query_when_testing==========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        if (node.isTryWithResources() && tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        if (node.isTryWithResources()) {
            ASTBlock body = node.getBody();
            if (body != null && body.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, body);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        } else if (node.isTryWithResources() && tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class);

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

        }

            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            ASTLocalVariableDeclaration varDecl = node.getVariableDeclaration();
            if (varDecl != null) {
                ASTVariableDeclaratorId varId = varDecl.getVarId();
                if (varId != null && !JavaRuleUtil.isExplicitUnusedVarName(varId.getName())) {
                    addViolation(data, body);
                }
            }
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            ASTLocalVariableDeclaration varDecl = node.getVariableDeclaration();
            if (varDecl != null) {
                ASTVariableDeclaratorId varId = varDecl.getVarId();
                if (varId != null && !JavaRuleUtil.isExplicitUnusedVarName(varId.getName())) {
                    addViolation(data, body);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            ASTLocalVariableDeclaration varDecl = node.getVariableDeclaration();
            if (varDecl != null) {
                ASTVariableDeclaratorId varId = varDecl.getVarId();
                if (varId != null && !JavaRuleUtil.isExplicitUnusedVarName(varId.getName())) {
                    addViolation(data, body);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports control statements whose body is empty, as well as empty initializers. The checked code constructs are the following: bodies of try statements、 finally clauses of try statements、 switch statements、 synchronized statements、 if statements、 loop statements: while, for, do .. while、initializers and blocks used as statements (for scoping).;

import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.codestyle;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class EmptyControlStatementRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public EmptyControlStatementRule() {
        super(ASTTryStatement.class, ASTSynchronizedStatement.class, ASTSwitchStatement.class, ASTBlock.class, ASTInitializer.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTIfStatement.class, ASTForeachStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTTryStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock tryBlock = node.getBody();
        if (tryBlock != null && tryBlock.getNumChildren() == 0 && !node.isTryWithResources()) {
            addViolation(data, tryBlock);
        }

        ASTFinallyClause finallyClause = node.getFinallyClause();
        if (finallyClause != null) {
            ASTBlock finallyBlock = finallyClause.getBody();
            if (finallyBlock != null && finallyBlock.getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, finallyBlock);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSynchronizedStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTSwitchStatement node, Object data) {
        if (node.getNumChildren() == 1) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTBlock node, Object data) {
        if (node.getParent() instanceof ASTBlock && node.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTInitializer node, Object data) {
        ASTBlock block = node.getBody();
        if (block != null && block.getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, block);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTIfStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement thenStmt = node.getThenBranch();
        if (thenStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) thenStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        } else if (thenStmt instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, thenStmt);
        }

        if (node.hasElse()) {
            ASTStatement elseStmt = node.getElseBranch();
            if (elseStmt instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) elseStmt).getNumChildren() == 0) {
                addViolation(data, elseStmt);
            } else if (elseStmt instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
                addViolation(data, elseStmt);
            }
        }

        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        ASTStatement body = node.getBody();
        if (body instanceof ASTBlock && ((ASTBlock) body).getNumChildren() == 0) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        } else if (body instanceof ASTEmptyStatement) {
            addViolation(data, body);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
